Talk

Ten Commandments for Parents

— Meng Ruo

The National Children's Year Implementation Committee has recently drafted ten commandments for parents and issued them to all provinces and cities for implementation. This is indeed a good way to seek happiness for children. Parents are the guardians of children, so if we want children to become successful, we must pay close attention to the education of children by their parents. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee's issuance of ten commandments for parents this time is also intended for this purpose.

The ten commandments for parents are drafted very appropriately. To be a responsible parent, you must have these ten kinds of confidence. If the parents in the family can implement these commandments, it will definitely be of great benefit to the education of children. Therefore, we hope that parents in general can pay considerable attention to these ten commandments.

We want to divide the ten commandments for parents into two categories: upbringing and education. (1) To the extent possible, children should be given an appropriate material environment; (2) The clothing, food, and housing provided to children should be hygienic as the first condition; (3) Children should be made to live a happy life all day long. These three items are methods of upbringing. (4) In order to cultivate good habits in children, parents should set an example; (5) Parents should be absolutely trustworthy to children; (6) When children have conflicts with us, parents should reflect on themselves and see if there are any mistakes; (7) Deceiving, intimidating, or corporal punishment is definitely not a method of educating children; (8) Children should be often encouraged to admit their mistakes and not blame others; (9) Cultivate children's habit of serving society, or make them do something beneficial to society every day; (10) Cultivate children's concept of patriotism, and start by making children use domestic products. These seven items are methods of education.

Regarding the educational aspect, setting an example is indeed the best way for parents to educate children. A parent who wants to cultivate good character in children should start with themselves and set an example for the children. How can parents who cannot set an example guide children to learn well? Cultivating children's habit of serving society and cultivating children's concept of patriotism are also two very important points that parents in the family cannot but pay attention to.

Regarding the upbringing aspect, giving children an appropriate material environment is very necessary. But this point is easy to achieve in some affluent families. If ordinary poor parents, they are unable to do so. Who doesn't like to make their children live a comfortable life? But in poor families, the material environment is very bad. Children naturally have to suffer. The way to improve is to hope that society can give them some help.

Finally, in addition to the ten commandments, we hope that the parents in the family will not regard children as private property and do not belittle the status of children. Everyone should take responsibility and use the most appropriate methods to protect our children.

The Fourth Son

— Changfeng

When the third son died, Mr. Li was playing cards at the club. Mr. Li was already approaching forty. If the first son was still alive, perhaps Mr. Li could have a grandson. Whenever there was a happy event at the homes of relatives and friends, Mr. Li would immediately burst into tears thinking of his first son. "What evil did I do in my previous life? What evil?" He would grab something and smash it, "I can't keep even one son, I can't keep him!" Because Mrs. Li's second pregnancy was also a miscarriage, according to the maid, it was also a male fetus, with all its hair grown.

But Mrs. Li was not as anxious as Mr. Li. She was deceiving herself: "We are not seventy or one hundred, we are still young, what are we afraid of! I am also a male belly." When Mrs. Li smiled and patted her belly, Mr. Li seemed to be relieved again, putting on a smile and answering his wife: "We don't do anything wrong, are we really afraid of not having a son?"

But Mr. Li was never as natural as his wife. As soon as he turned around, the son problem twisted his heart again. It was at that time, under the urging of his wife and the persuasion of friends, that Mr. Li learned to play cards. He went to the club every day, putting the son problem and his thoughts on the white board to get rich.

In the year he turned forty, Mrs. Li became pregnant again. During that time, he played smoothly every day at the club. Knowing this news, he happily said:

"When luck comes, everything goes smoothly. It's not too late to have a son at forty!"

Mrs. Li naturally also smiled, as if she was already holding her son, answering her husband with certainty: "Isn't it? Jiang Taigong didn't marry until he was eighty! I am also a male belly, what are we afraid of? Don't let people know, you can make a small fortune at the card table!" (According to local customs, getting married or having a wife pregnant can guarantee victory when playing cards.)

Mr. Li really played smoothly every day. He was extremely happy, thinking in his heart all the time, "It must be a son! It will definitely be a son! Isn't this card game a sign?"

On the day of his birthday, his friends came to his house to congratulate him. They discovered that Mrs. Li's belly was as high as a small hill, wearing a cheongsam with unbuttoned buttons, walking in and out to greet the guests. While drinking happily, a friend who played cards with Mr. Li every day said; "Old Li has double happiness, no wonder his card playing is so smooth. Old Li, you are hiding it from us, do you think you should be punished or not?"

"Punish! Punish!" Everyone clapped and echoed.

"Punish! Punish!" Mr. Li was so proud, "I'll offer everyone a glass of wine, how about punishing one hundred red eggs?"

Mr. Li raised his neck, lifted his glass and drank it all in one gulp, clasping his fists with both hands and waving them on the table, almost as happy as when his eldest son was one month old. He got drunk that day.

A month later, Mrs. Li was in labor, and sure enough, it was a son.

Because Mr. Li had a son in his old age, his friends discussed having a big celebration when the baby was one month old. They came up with many tricks at the card table, and those who could sing prepared to sing, and those who couldn't asked the hall to sing; and for good luck, they entrusted the child to a friend with many children, and also prepared to hold a ceremony on the day of the one-month celebration.

But the third son did not grow up, and was often sick. One day, Mr. Li was playing cards at the club. The servant at home said that the child was seriously ill and asked him to go back. That day was one week away from the one-month celebration.

The child would not drink milk, nor would he cry. The doctors who were invited all shook their heads. They did not dare to give medicine to the child who was more than twenty days old, and even advised Mr. Li to invite an experienced child scholar girl to try. (Child scholar girls often used inexplicable folk methods to treat diseases.)

But those effective folk methods were not effective. The child only had a breath rolling in his throat, and he could no longer receive medicine. Two days before the one-month celebration, he ended his life, pushing Mr. Li from the peak of hope into a cold ice cellar. Mrs. Li also said disappointedly: "Are we really destined not to have children?"

Mr. Li's diet and sleep were irregular for several days, so naturally he did not go to the club to play cards. Those friends also dropped from the hot expectation point to the freezing point, thinking of ways to comfort Mr. Li as if it were their own business. Mr. Li could only walk around the room like a madman. When he grabbed something in his hand, he smashed it to pieces on the ground, as if that thing was the one that put his son in the ground.

"What evil did I do in my previous life! What evil!" He could only shout like this: "Those debt collectors! Unending debts! Unending debts!"

Mrs. Li also lost the energy of "I am a male belly" to comfort her husband. Three sons had not kept one, what was the use of "male belly"?

Afterwards, Mr. Li suddenly figured it out. If it was destined that he would not have a son, it could not be recovered by force. He still went to the club to play cards every day, or pulled his wife and friends to listen to operas. When he was happy, he would go to Hangzhou and Suzhou to stay for ten days and a half months. He seriously said to his wife from time to time: "It is destined that we will not have a son, let's enjoy ourselves! When our legs are stretched out, everything will belong to others. It is only bitter to be poor in old age!"

But the fourth son had taken root in his wife's belly again, and was rising day by day, piling up in front of Mr. Li like a small hill.

"Debt collector! Debt collector!" Mr. Li scolded as if he was arguing with someone. But the latent thought was also growing in his mind. It would not be more than two if it was not one, it would not be more than three if it was not two. Now it was the fourth one, perhaps he was destined to raise a son in his old age.

As his wife's belly rose day by day, Mr. Li became more and more uneasy. He was only living in contradictory thoughts, looking at his wife's "male belly" piled up in front of him...

Small Electric Bulb Industry (Part 1)

— Voice

(Industry Survey) The electric bulb industry is divided into several types. There are large electric bulbs specifically for lighting; automobile bulbs specifically for cars; and small electric bulbs (i.e., beads) specifically for flashlights. Large-scale manufacturers naturally produce all kinds, but smaller ones mostly specialize in one or two types. Among these types of electric bulb industries, the capital for manufacturing small electric bulbs is the most flexible. It is said that some small factories can start manufacturing with a cash flow of only three to five hundred. Because the small electric bulb industry has the characteristics of a home craft, it is relatively easy to start. However, the manufacturing process of small electric bulbs is not much different from that of large electric bulbs. Don't underestimate it; when a small electric bulb is successfully manufactured and can light up in a flashlight, it truly goes through many steps and procedures involving numerous workers.

Now, I will present a concept of the work process of small electric bulb manufacturing, which is often overlooked.

Page 19

(1) Winding Tungsten Wire and Tungsten Bead Copper Wire: Winding tungsten wire is the first step. This work can be done by a lady. Because the tungsten winding machine uses a motor, even with a hand-cranked machine, tens of thousands can be wound per day. The work is light and the wage is high. These raw materials all come from abroad. It is said that German and Italian products are the best, and Japan also manufactures them. The price is very high, calculated by the meter. However, it is different for copper wire with beads; because it has different thicknesses, it is calculated by weight (pounds). The workers who make the beads hang the two ends of the copper wire on a bow, hold the back of the bow with one hand, and hold a colored glass rod with the other hand, placing it on an open flame to melt it. They wind a circle around the copper wire, and after it sticks, it looks like a small bead. Each copper wire needs to have thirty-five or six such beads. These workers are mostly female workers from elsewhere, and their wages are calculated per copper wire. About three jiao (a unit of Chinese currency) in legal tender is paid for every hundred wires completed. One can complete about one hundred thirty or forty wires per day. (To be continued)

Suzhou People (19)

— By Gu Wenzong

Liya: My attitude is not sour, thank you for caring about a stranger. If you want to leave this seat voluntarily, then please do so.

Jinghong: Mr. Zhao, it would be okay to come back if you can't find a seat elsewhere.

Dajun: Yes! Goodbye, ladies.

Jinghong: Good, thank you for giving up this seat for my friend to sit.

Dajun: It's nothing, you don't have to be so polite, goodbye.

Jinghong: Goodbye! (Footsteps receding) Miss Jin, sit across from me and let's talk.

Liya: Look at his attire, it's completely the typical slick character you often see in American movies, with none of the demeanor of a proper English gentleman!

Jinghong: He has been to America, so naturally he will pick up some habits of fashionable American youth. Although his clothing is a bit modern, he still understands the rules of wearing clothes and doesn't dress haphazardly like those who don't understand how to wear Western clothes.

Liya: How do you know he has been to America?

Jinghong: He revealed it inadvertently just now.

Opening "Qin Liangyu"

The Ming Dynasty was in danger and the country was falling apart. Unexpectedly, there was a female general in Sichuan. Qin Liangyu, versed in both literature and martial arts. A sigh for a heroine who is not a professional soldier. Tracing back to her, when she was young, she received her father's teachings. The whole family trained as defenders. The brothers and sisters shared strategies. But she was a woman who did not yield to men. Furthermore, the Stone Pillar sought a phoenix spouse. Heroic sons and daughters united in marriage. A worthy couple of men and women. A generation of heroes passed on their famous name. Advise your husband, a good man should repay his aspirations. You must give your life to save the country and establish meritorious service. Imagine the battlefields filled with swords and halberds. The military orders are strict for the Baigan soldiers. At that time, the situation was complicated and changeable. The two defended against the enemy and no one could stop them. Banners fluttered and drums roared with mighty power. They were worthy of being called the wife of the lady general. How hateful that the eunuchs abused their power and trapped the people in hell. Qiancheng died and went to the underworld. Look at her, wearing mourning clothes and going to the army. She has the ambition to restore the Ming, but her wish has not been fulfilled. Fortunately, she was ordered to come to the capital to take over her post. Changing her clothes and removing her hairpins. A red-clad rider on a peach-colored horse. Green sleeves lining the clouds in the willow camp. I only saw her, the Sichuan brocade robe stained with battle blood. Rushing on the royal road to show loyalty. She also relieved the national crisis with her family wealth, generously donating money without hesitation. This is the uniqueness of the spiritual essence of heaven and earth. The heroic spirit of the mountains and rivers strengthens this person. Even admire her. The gift robe praised and passed down through the ages. Receiving the honor and commendation of the country. Furthermore, there are auspicious omens revealing the great virtue. A family of loyalty, righteousness, and happy martyrdom. Later, the treacherous officials dismissed her from her post. The collapse and disintegration of the country was a painful demise for the Ming. But I am filled with melancholy and worry as I reflect on the past. I only hope that we can work together to save the national soul. It is truly just talking about war on paper.

Movies

The Making of "The Good Earth"

— Lai

There have been significant changes regarding Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer's film "The Good Earth," which is about China. This new film recently began production in Hollywood.

Originally, the director intended for all the actors in this film to be Chinese and to speak Chinese. Now, there have been significant changes. Foreign actors are playing important roles, and the dialogue has been changed to English. Paul Muni plays Wang Lung, a Chinese farmer, and Iuice Ralner—now an Austrian star in Hollywood—plays Alan, Wang Lung's wife.

Paul Muni previously spent time with several overseas Chinese farmers in the Sacramento Valley to learn their personalities, farming techniques, and various movements. Ms. Ralner has also recently learned the movements and attitudes she needs to know. The director of this film is Fleming, and the famous European cinematographer Karl Freund is the cinematographer for this film.

American film circles have rumored that Paul Muni has mastered a lot of Chinese characters and can realistically express the character's personality, as well as the postures and gestures of Chinese farmers and other characteristics.

A Chinese-style avenue is now visible along the road from Los Angeles to Chatsworth City. A large space is used for the film "The Good Earth"; hundreds of Chinese people have been hired (not speaking) and are currently working in several miles of mountainous terrain, which includes farming tools from rural North China for irrigation of farmland.

Fields of wheat and rice have already been planted. The second half of the film's production must wait until the rice and wheat have grown. A Chinese-style town was specially designed and built by Chinese architects.

The screenplay for "The Good Earth" was adapted by Ms. Frances Marion and director George Hill. The assistant writers include Ms. Betty Wang, a former employee of the Shanghai Continental Daily, and Maurice Liu, who is from Shanghai.

The Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer "The Good Earth" crew arrived in Shanghai in January 1935 and spent six months filming in China. The main figures were Frank Messenger, Charles Haws, and George Clarke. George Hill committed suicide after returning to the United States. After they arrived in China, they shot a lot of outdoor scenes, mainly in Beijing, Shanghai, and Suzhou.

When the Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer crew left Shanghai, they entrusted foreign lawyer Ouleman to help find actors in China. They posted advertisements in Shanghai and Tianjin, and hundreds of people applied, but only fifteen were not rejected. However, when the results of the trials of these fifteen people in Shanghai were sent to Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer, they were considered unsatisfactory, and they had no choice but to use foreign actors.

Since the Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer crew left China and returned to the United States, Mr. Du Tingxiu, the representative of the Chinese government, has followed them and is stationed in Hollywood to monitor everything. The Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer authorities also asked him to stay there until the film is completed.

"Torrent of Desire"

Playing in Nanjing

Jin Cheng to Open Air Conditioning

And Add New Air Conditioners

The first-run cinemas in Shanghai that show Western films, such as Da Guangming, Cathay, and Nanjing, all have air conditioning, but among the theaters that show domestic films, only Jin Cheng has air conditioning. Jin Cheng's air conditioner was installed by air conditioning expert York Company; last summer, it won excellent public opinion. Everyone said that it was comparable to Da Guangming's air conditioning equipment. Now, in order to strive for excellence, they are sparing no expense and adding new air conditioners to make the air in the entire theater not dry or humid, but just right. They are currently working day and night to install it, and it will be open soon. As the weather gets warmer, this may be a piece of news that all Shanghai movie fans would like to hear.
